`build_task_context(prior_results: list[TaskResult], *, start_commit: str = \"\", compress_threshold: int = 3) -> str`\n- Behavior:\n  - Returns `\"\"` if `prior_results` is empty.\n  - Builds markdown starting with `## Prior Task Context`.\n  - Uses full summaries for all prior tasks if result count is `<= compress_threshold`.\n  - Uses progressive summarization if count exceeds threshold.\n  - Appends:\n    - `### Gate Outcomes`\n      - one line per task: `- T01.01: pass`\n    - `### Remediation History`\n      - only for tasks with `reimbursement_amount > 0`\n    - optional git diff section via `get_git_diff_context(start_commit)`\n\n#### `get_git_diff_context`\n- Signature:\n  - `get_git_diff_context(start_commit: str) -> str`\n- Behavior:\n  - Runs `git diff --stat <start_commit>`\n  - Returns markdown section:\n    - `### Git Changes Since Sprint Start`\n    - fenced code block with diff stat\n  - Returns empty string on:\n    - non-zero git exit\n    - empty stdout\n    - `FileNotFoundError`\n    - `TimeoutExpired`\n    - `OSError`\n\n#### `compress_context_summary`\n- Signature:\n  - `compress_context_summary(results: list[TaskResult], *, keep_recent: int = 3) -> str`\n- Behavior:\n  - Returns `\"\"` for empty input\n  - If `len(results) > keep_recent`:\n    - older items go under `#### Earlier Tasks (compressed)`\n    - uses `to_context_summary(verbose=False)`\n  - recent items go under `#### Recent Tasks`\n    - uses `to_context_summary(verbose=True)`\n\n#### Evidence about wiring\nI searched for call sites of `build_task_context(` and only found the function definition in this file.\nAlso, `_run_task_subprocess()` in sprint executor currently builds prompt as:\n- task id\n- task title\n- phase file\n- task description\n\nIt does not currently append context built from prior `TaskResult`s.\n\nSo:\n- context builder exists\n- `TaskResult` supports context serialization\n- progressive summarization exists\n- gate outcomes and remediation history are included\n- git diff context exists\n- but current per-task runner does not appear to inject it yet\n\n## 2. `GateResultQueue` APIs\n\n### `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/trailing_gate.py`\n\n#### `TrailingGateResult`\n- Signature:\n  - `TrailingGateResult(step_id: str, passed: bool, evaluation_ms: float, failure_reason: str | None = None)`\n- Meaning of `evaluation_ms`:\n  - measured wall-clock duration in milliseconds for gate evaluation\n  - computed as:\n    - `(time.monotonic() - start) * 1000`\n  - immediate no-gate success uses `0.0`\n  - exception fallback also uses `0.0`\n\n#### `GateResultQueue`\n- Signature:\n  - `GateResultQueue()`\n- Methods:\n  - `put(self, result: TrailingGateResult) -> None`\n  - `drain(self) -> list[TrailingGateResult]`\n  - `pending_count(self) -> int`\n- Behavior:\n  - thread-safe queue wrapper\n  - `drain()` is non-blocking and empties currently available results\n  - `pending_count()` uses queue size\n\n#### `TrailingGateRunner`\n- Signature:\n  - `TrailingGateRunner(result_queue: GateResultQueue | None = None)`\n- Property:\n  - `result_queue(self) -> GateResultQueue`\n- Methods:\n  - `submit(self, step: Step, gate_check: Callable[[Path, GateCriteria], tuple[bool, str | None]] = gate_passed) -> None`\n  - `drain(self) -> list[TrailingGateResult]`\n  - `wait_for_pending(self, timeout: float = 30.0) -> list[TrailingGateResult]`\n  - `cancel(self) -> None`\n- Property:\n  - `pending_count(self) -> int`\n- Behavior details:\n  - if `step.gate is None`, `submit()` immediately enqueues:\n    - `TrailingGateResult(step_id=step.id, passed=True, evaluation_ms=0.0, failure_reason=None)`\n  - otherwise spawns daemon thread\n  - on success, enqueues measured result\n  - on exception, enqueues failed result with:\n    - `passed=False`\n    - `evaluation_ms=0.0`\n    - `failure_reason=\"Gate evaluation raised an exception\"`\n\n#### `resolve_gate_mode`\n- Signature:\n  - `resolve_gate_mode(scope: GateScope, config_gate_mode: GateMode = GateMode.BLOCKING, grace_period: int = 0) -> GateMode`\n- Rules:\n  - release -> always `BLOCKING`\n  - milestone -> configurable\n  - task -> `TRAILING` if `grace_period > 0`, else `BLOCKING`\n\n## 5. failure_reason: str | None = None)`\n\n`evaluation_ms` semantics:\n- float in milliseconds\n- measured only for actual async gate evaluation path\n- calculated around `gate_check(step.output_file, `build_task_context(prior_results: list[TaskResult], *, start_commit: str = \"\", compress_threshold: int = 3) -> str`\n- Behavior:\n  - Returns `\"\"` if `prior_results` is empty.\n  - Builds markdown starting with `## Prior Task Context`.\n  - Uses full summaries for all prior tasks if result count is `<= compress_threshold`.\n  - Uses progressive summarization if count exceeds threshold.\n  - Appends:\n    - `### Gate Outcomes`\n      - one line per task: `- T01.01: pass`\n    - `### Remediation History`\n      - only for tasks with `reimbursement_amount > 0`\n    - optional git diff section via `get_git_diff_context(start_commit)`\n\n#### `get_git_diff_context`\n- Signature:\n  - `get_git_diff_context(start_commit: str) -> str`\n- Behavior:\n  - Runs `git diff --stat <start_commit>`\n  - Returns markdown section:\n    - `### Git Changes Since Sprint Start`\n    - fenced code block with diff stat\n  - Returns empty string on:\n    - non-zero git exit\n    - empty stdout\n    - `FileNotFoundError`\n    - `TimeoutExpired`\n    - `OSError`\n\n#### `compress_context_summary`\n- Signature:\n  - `compress_context_summary(results: list[TaskResult], *, keep_recent: int = 3) -> str`\n- Behavior:\n  - Returns `\"\"` for empty input\n  - If `len(results) > keep_recent`:\n    - older items go under `#### Earlier Tasks (compressed)`\n    - uses `to_context_summary(verbose=False)`\n  - recent items go under `#### Recent Tasks`\n    - uses `to_context_summary(verbose=True)`\n\n#### Evidence about wiring\nI searched for call sites of `build_task_context(` and only found the function definition in this file.\nAlso, `_run_task_subprocess()` in sprint executor currently builds prompt as:\n- task id\n- task title\n- phase file\n- task description\n\nIt does not currently append context built from prior `TaskResult`s.\n\nSo:\n- context builder exists\n- `TaskResult` supports context serialization\n- progressive summarization exists\n- gate outcomes and remediation history are included\n- git diff context exists\n- but current per-task runner does not appear to inject it yet\n\n## 2. `GateResultQueue` APIs\n\n### `/config/workspace/SuperClaude_Framework/src/superclaude/cli/pipeline/trailing_gate.py`\n\n#### `TrailingGateResult`\n- Signature:\n  - `TrailingGateResult(step_id: str, passed: bool, evaluation_ms: float, failure_reason: str | None = None)`\n- Meaning of `evaluation_ms`:\n  - measured wall-clock duration in milliseconds for gate evaluation\n  - computed as:\n    - `(time.monotonic() - start) * 1000`\n  - immediate no-gate success uses `0.0`\n  - exception fallback also uses `0.0`\n\n#### `GateResultQueue`\n- Signature:\n  - `GateResultQueue()`\n- Methods:\n  - `put(self, result: TrailingGateResult) -> None`\n  - `drain(self) -> list[TrailingGateResult]`\n  - `pending_count(self) -> int`\n- Behavior:\n  - thread-safe queue wrapper\n  - `drain()` is non-blocking and empties currently available results\n  - `pending_count()` uses queue size\n\n#### `TrailingGateRunner`\n- Signature:\n  - `TrailingGateRunner(result_queue: GateResultQueue | None = None)`\n- Property:\n  - `result_queue(self) -> GateResultQueue`\n- Methods:\n  - `submit(self, step: Step, gate_check: Callable[[Path, GateCriteria], tuple[bool, str | None]] = gate_passed) -> None`\n  - `drain(self) -> list[TrailingGateResult]`\n  - `wait_for_pending(self, timeout: float = 30.0) -> list[TrailingGateResult]`\n  - `cancel(self) -> None`\n- Property:\n  - `pending_count(self) -> int`\n- Behavior details:\n  - if `step.gate is None`, `submit()` immediately enqueues:\n    - `TrailingGateResult(step_id=step.id, passed=True, evaluation_ms=0.0, failure_reason=None)`\n  - otherwise spawns daemon thread\n  - on success, enqueues measured result\n  - on exception, enqueues failed result with:\n    - `passed=False`\n    - `evaluation_ms=0.0`\n    - `failure_reason=\"Gate evaluation raised an exception\"`\n\n#### `resolve_gate_mode`\n- Signature:\n  - `resolve_gate_mode(scope: GateScope, config_gate_mode: GateMode = GateMode.BLOCKING, grace_period: int = 0) -> GateMode`\n- Rules:\n  - release -> always `BLOCKING`\n  - milestone -> configurable\n  - task -> `TRAILING` if `grace_period > 0`, else `BLOCKING`\n\n## 5.    \"\"\"3 threads putting concurrently â€” no result loss.\"\"\"\n        q = GateResultQueue()\n        items_per_thread = 50\n\n        def producer(prefix: str):\n            for i in
